** Prompt

Run this Cabinet job: Weekly Architecture Scan.

Review the Cabinet, docs, and recent changes for architectural drift. Summarize risks, stale docs, confusing UX, and concrete next actions.

** Output
#+begin_src text
No blocking defects showed up in the current uncommitted Evil integration. The Cabinet-specific tests passed, the changed Elisp files byte-compile cleanly, and the real problems are architectural drift and discoverability.

**Findings**
[P2] Cabinet has two competing “primary surface” contracts.
Files: [specs/architecture.org](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/specs/architecture.org:76), [specs/cabinet-org-os.org](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/specs/cabinet-org-os.org:201), [docs/cabinet.org](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/docs/cabinet.org:9), [README.md](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/README.md:21)
Impact: contributors can land new work on the wrong surface, and the docs already give opposite guidance depending on which file they read first.
Reasoning: `specs/architecture.org` still says `ogent-cabinet-status` is the operational entry point, while the deeper Cabinet spec, README, user guide, and tests treat `ogent-cabinet-home` as the main surface.
Fix direction: choose one canonical entry surface and align the rest. The smallest coherent move is updating `specs/architecture.org` to match Home-first behavior.

[P2] The storage contract advertises directories that the runtime does not use.
Files: [specs/cabinet-org-os.org](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/specs/cabinet-org-os.org:50), [lisp/ogent-cabinet.el](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/lisp/ogent-cabinet.el:31), [lisp/ogent-cabinet.el](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/lisp/ogent-cabinet.el:687), [lisp/ogent-cabinet-runner.el](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/lisp/ogent-cabinet-runner.el:109)
Impact: future Cabinet features can fork persistence across “official” paths with no obvious failure until users cannot find transcripts or job state.
Reasoning: scaffold creates `.agents/.conversations` and `.jobs`, but live session reads and writes go through `.agents/<slug>/sessions/`, and `.agents/.conversations` is explicitly hidden from discovery.
Fix direction: either remove the unused scaffold dirs and spec mentions, or wire them into the live model. Current code already points toward per-agent `sessions/` as canonical.

[P2] Jobs are documented as a first-class workflow, but the primary UI does not expose them.
Files: [docs/cabinet.org](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/docs/cabinet.org:67), [README.md](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/README.md:95), [lisp/ui/ogent-ui-cabinet.el](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/lisp/ui/ogent-ui-cabinet.el:360), [lisp/ui/ogent-ui-cabinet.el](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/lisp/ui/ogent-ui-cabinet.el:1024)
Impact: the “first 10 minutes” flow tells users to open `ogent-cabinet-jobs`, but Home and Status never advertise a jobs surface. That is a UX seam, not a power-user feature.
Reasoning: `ogent-cabinet-jobs` exists and is tested, but Home navigation only surfaces agents, tasks, conversations, search, apps, and graph. README keybindings omit jobs entirely.
Fix direction: add a Jobs entry point from Home or Status, or rewrite the onboarding flow around agent profiles if that is the intended path.

[P3] The new Evil support is correct, but it adds another recurring sync point.
Files: [lisp/ogent-cabinet-status.el](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/lisp/ogent-cabinet-status.el:491), [lisp/ui/ogent-ui-cabinet.el](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/lisp/ui/ogent-ui-cabinet.el:2019)
Impact: every new Cabinet mode now needs updates in two Evil registration helpers. Low blast radius, steady maintenance tax.
Reasoning: the local patch duplicates mode registration and overriding-map setup across the status module and the richer UI module.
Fix direction: centralize Cabinet Evil registration behind one shared helper or one shared mode list.

**Stale Docs**
`docs/cabinet.org` still says the graph includes `issue-link` nodes at [docs/cabinet.org](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/docs/cabinet.org:94), while the graph projection and UI use `issue` nodes in [lisp/ogent-cabinet.el](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/lisp/ogent-cabinet.el:964) and [lisp/ogent-cabinet-status.el](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/lisp/ogent-cabinet-status.el:287).

The current Evil patch changes the lived behavior of Cabinet buffers, but there is no matching note in the Cabinet or Doom docs near the keybinding sections in [docs/cabinet.org](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/docs/cabinet.org:97) and [docs/doom-emacs.md](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/docs/doom-emacs.md:118).

**Next Actions**
1. Create a doc-alignment bead to unify `specs/architecture.org`, `specs/cabinet-org-os.org`, `docs/cabinet.org`, and README on one Cabinet entry surface.
2. Create a storage-contract cleanup bead to remove or justify `.agents/.conversations` and `.jobs`, then document the canonical transcript location.
3. Create a jobs-discoverability bead to expose jobs from Home/Status or change the onboarding docs to match the real navigation path.
4. Fold Evil setup into shared Cabinet UI plumbing, then add one short Doom/Evil note when that patch lands.

Validation: reviewed the local Cabinet diff in [lisp/ogent-cabinet-status.el](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/lisp/ogent-cabinet-status.el:491), [lisp/ui/ogent-ui-cabinet.el](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/lisp/ui/ogent-ui-cabinet.el:2019), [test/ogent-cabinet-status-tests.el](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/test/ogent-cabinet-status-tests.el:137), and [test/ui/ogent-ui-cabinet-tests.el](/Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent/test/ui/ogent-ui-cabinet-tests.el:580). Ran targeted ERT for the two Cabinet test files, `29/29` passed. Byte-compiled the two changed Elisp files cleanly.

# Gas Town Worker Context

> **Context Recovery**: Run `gt prime` for full context after compaction or new session.

## The Propulsion Principle (GUPP)

**If you find work on your hook, YOU RUN IT.**

No confirmation. No waiting. No announcements. The hook having work IS the assignment.
This is physics, not politeness. Gas Town is a steam engine - you are a piston.

**Failure mode we're preventing:**
- Agent starts with work on hook
- Agent announces itself and waits for human to say "ok go"
- Human is AFK / trusting the engine to run
- Work sits idle. The whole system stalls.

## Startup Protocol

1. Check your hook: `gt mol status`
2. If work is hooked → EXECUTE (no announcement, no waiting)
3. If hook empty → Check mail: `gt mail inbox`
4. Still nothing? Wait for user instructions

## Key Commands

- `gt prime` - Get full role context (run after compaction)
- `gt mol status` - Check your hooked work
- `gt mail inbox` - Check for messages
- `bd ready` - Find available work (no blockers)

## Session Close Protocol

Before signaling completion:
1. git status (check what changed)
2. git add <files> (stage code changes)
3. git commit -m "..." (commit code)
4. git push (push to remote)
5. `gt done` (submit to merge queue and exit)

**Polecats MUST call `gt done` - this submits work and exits the session.**

#+title: Cabinet User Guide

* What Cabinet Is

Cabinet is an Org-backed local knowledge OS for AI-team work inside Emacs. A
Cabinet root is a directory with =index.org= plus agent, job, conversation,
task, app, import, and relationship records stored as Org files.

The main command is =M-x ogent-cabinet-home=. It opens a single operational UI
with metadata, health counts, navigation, recent activity, and work needing
attention. Failed work is shown in Cabinet Home and on the task board.

* Durable Layout

#+begin_example
cabinet-root/
  index.org
  imports/
  .agents/
    editor/
      persona.org
      inbox.org
      schedule.org
      jobs/
        weekly-review.org
      memory/
        context.org
        decisions.org
        learnings.org
      sessions/
        20260504T090000-weekly-review.org
#+end_example

Org is the durable source of truth. Commands edit property drawers and body
text in those Org files. Manual edits remain part of the record.

* First 10 Minutes

1. Create a Cabinet:

   #+begin_src emacs-lisp
   (ogent-cabinet-scaffold "~/cabinet/acme" "Acme Cabinet" :kind "root")
,   #+end_src

2. Open the operating surface:

   #+begin_example
   M-x ogent-cabinet-home
   #+end_example

3. Create an agent:

   #+begin_example
   M-x ogent-cabinet-create-agent
   #+end_example

   Fill in name, slug, role, provider, model, workspace, tags, and persona.

4. Add a recurring job:

   #+begin_example
   M-x ogent-cabinet-create-job
   #+end_example

   The job is written under =.agents/<slug>/jobs/<job-id>.org=.

5. Run the job:

   Open =M-x ogent-cabinet-jobs=, move to the job, press =R=.

6. Inspect the transcript:

   Open =M-x ogent-cabinet-conversations= and press =RET= on the new run.
   The detail buffer shows metadata, prompt, output, tool blocks, errors,
   app links, duration, and source Org.

7. Search the Cabinet:

   Use =M-x ogent-cabinet-search=. Empty queries show an empty state. Search
   can filter by kind, agent, status, tag, and archive state from Lisp callers.

8. Open generated apps:

   Use =M-x ogent-cabinet-apps=. Each =index.html= below the Cabinet root is
   listed with label, path, modified time, and inferred owner when possible.

9. Check the task board:

   Use =M-x ogent-cabinet-tasks=. Lanes are Inbox, Needs Reply, Running,
   Scheduled, Just Finished, Stale, and Archive.

10. Inspect relationships:

    Use =M-x ogent-cabinet-status=. The graph includes cabinet, agent, job,
    session, app, issue-link, and Gas Town hook nodes when available.

* Keybindings

Main ogent dispatch bindings:

| Key | Command |
|-----+---------|
| =C-c . j= / =SPC o j= | =ogent-cabinet-home= |
| =C-c . K= / =SPC o K= | =ogent-cabinet-status= |
| =C-c . y= / =SPC o y= | =ogent-cabinet-agents= |
| =C-c . Y= / =SPC o Y= | =ogent-cabinet-agent= |
| =C-c . I= / =SPC o I= | =ogent-cabinet-tasks= |
| =C-c . O= / =SPC o O= | =ogent-cabinet-conversations= |
| =C-c . V= / =SPC o V= | =ogent-cabinet-search= |
| =C-c . W= / =SPC o W= | =ogent-cabinet-apps= |
| =C-c . X= / =SPC o X= | =ogent-cabinet-create-agent= |
| =C-c . Z= / =SPC o Z= | =ogent-cabinet-create-job= |

Cabinet Home:

| Key | Action |
|-----+--------|
| =RET= | Visit the item at point |
| =g= | Refresh |
| =q= | Quit |
| =a= | Agents |
| =t= | Tasks |
| =c= | Conversations |
| =s= | Search |
| =A= | Apps |
| =G= | Graph/status |
| =e= | Edit Cabinet metadata |
| =n= / =p= | Move between actionable rows |

Agent profile:

| Key | Action |
|-----+--------|
| =RET= / =v= | Visit the file or record at point |
| =c= | Compose and run the agent manually |
| =e= | Edit identity metadata in the property drawer |
| =R= | Run the job at point or retry the conversation at point |
| =q= | Quit |

Jobs:

| Key | Action |
|-----+--------|
| =RET= | Visit source Org |
| =P= | Edit the job prompt/body |
| =e= | Edit job metadata |
| =R= | Run the job now |
| =T= | Enable or disable |
| =A= | Archive |
| =g= | Refresh |

Task board:

| Key | Action |
|-----+--------|
| =RET= | Visit source Org |
| =R= | Run or retry |
| =A= | Archive |
| =U= | Unarchive |
| =e= | Edit metadata |
| =f= | Filter |
| =g= | Refresh |

* Importing Existing Artifacts

=ogent-cabinet-import-artifacts= imports =.md=, =.html=, and =.txt= files from
a source folder into =imports/*.org= records. Original files are kept by
default. Markdown headings are converted to Org headings. HTML is preserved in
an Org source block.

Migration limits:

- Import is conservative and does not delete originals.
- Ambiguous metadata becomes a normal import record.
- Agent and job creation from imported metadata is intentionally narrow; use
  =ogent-cabinet-create-agent= and =ogent-cabinet-create-job= when the source
  does not identify a clear agent or job.
- Imported files become Cabinet Org records, but external links and rich HTML
  behavior may need manual cleanup.

* Doom Example

#+begin_src emacs-lisp
(use-package! ogent
  :defer t
  :commands (ogent-mode
             ogent-cabinet-home
             ogent-cabinet-status
             ogent-cabinet-agents
             ogent-cabinet-agent
             ogent-cabinet-tasks
             ogent-cabinet-conversations
             ogent-cabinet-search
             ogent-cabinet-apps
             ogent-cabinet-create-agent
             ogent-cabinet-create-job)
  :init
  (setq ogent-enable-doom-bindings t
        ogent-doom-prefix "o")
  :config
  (ogent-setup-doom-bindings)
  (ogent-global-mode 1))
,#+end_src

---
name: code-review-checklist
description: Systematic code review workflow adapted from Michaela Greiler's code-review-checklist. Use when reviewing pull requests, merge requests, diffs, patches, staged changes, or local changes for correctness, bugs, error handling, dependencies, security/privacy, performance, usability/accessibility, ethics, tests, readability, documentation, and expert-review gaps.
---

# Code Review Checklist

Use this as a review operating mode, not a form to dump into the answer. The goal is to find real risks in the change and report them with enough precision that the author can act immediately.

This skill is host-portable. It uses only `SKILL.md` plus Markdown references, which works for Claude Code and Codex. Follow the active host's instructions for tool use, inline comments, and final-answer format.

## Review Contract

- Lead with findings for code-review requests. Order them by severity.
- Ground every finding in a concrete file and line, or in a specific changed behavior when a line is not enough.
- Report confirmed defects, release risks, missing coverage, and important open questions. Skip generic advice.
- Prefer root-cause findings: identify the broken contract, invariant, state transition, trust boundary, or failure mode.
- Do not approve by checklist completion alone. Check the risky paths, then state residual risk.
- If no issues are found, say that directly and mention unrun tests or areas not inspected.
- Use host-native inline review comments only when requested or when the host's standing instructions require them.

## Workflow

1. Establish intent. Read the user request, PR description, issue links, tests, docs, and migration/config notes.
2. Map the diff. Identify changed entry points, shared APIs, persistence, generated files, vendored files, and cross-module contracts.
3. Prioritize high-risk paths. Start with auth, permissions, secrets, user data, payments, migrations, concurrency, retries, external APIs, and data loss.
4. Apply the checklist lenses below. For a deep or formal review, load `references/checklist.md`.
5. Validate with targeted commands when the project context makes them clear. If commands are expensive or unavailable, say what was not run.
6. Produce the review. Findings first, then open questions, then a short test/coverage note.

## Checklist Lenses

Scan each lens quickly during normal review. Expand only the lenses touched by the diff.

- Implementation and architecture: intent, simplicity, abstraction level, modularity, local reuse, patterns, dependency shape.
- Logic and edge cases: invalid inputs, unusual ordering, boundary values, partial failure, concurrency, time, idempotency.
- Error handling and observability: actionable errors, retry/fallback behavior, logging level, debugging value, noisy or secret-bearing logs.
- Dependencies, docs, and compatibility: new packages/services, config drift, documentation, migration path, callers and downstream consumers.
- Security and privacy: authz/authn, injection, validation, escaping, secret exposure, encryption, user data handling, third-party data.
- Performance: algorithmic complexity, allocation/IO hot spots, cache behavior, query fanout, render churn, scalability limits.
- Usability, accessibility, and API design: intuitive flows, accessible UI, clear API contract, discoverability, documented behavior.
- Ethics and abuse: user data use, manipulation, harassment/abuse paths, exclusion, unfair impact, AI/ML bias.
- Testing and testability: meaningful automated coverage, edge cases, real integrations where feasible, determinism, observability for failures.
- Readability and maintainability: names, control flow, file placement, comments, dead/commented code, data-flow clarity.
- Expert review: security, privacy, accessibility, infra, legal, data science, or team ownership sign-off when risk crosses domains.

## Output Shape

For findings, use this shape unless the host has stricter review rules:

```markdown
[P1] Short imperative title
File: path/to/file.ext:123
Impact: What can break, leak, regress, or confuse users.
Reasoning: Why this follows from the code.
Fix direction: The smallest correct design-level fix.
```

Severity guide:

- `P0`: ships a security issue, data loss/corruption, outage, or unusable core path.
- `P1`: likely production bug, serious regression, broken contract, or missing high-risk coverage.
- `P2`: correctness, maintainability, or coverage problem with limited blast radius.
- `P3`: polish or cleanup that is useful but not release-blocking.

## Reference

Load `references/checklist.md` when the user asks for a comprehensive checklist pass, when reviewing a large or risky change, or when you need a domain-by-domain prompt to avoid missing categories.

 succeeded in 0ms:
#+title: ogent Architectural Constraints

* Design Philosophy

ogent treats language models as Unix tools: they take structured input, produce structured output, and compose with everything else in Emacs. The user remains in the loop, wielding the tool rather than supervising an agent.

** Core Principles

*** Text as Interface
Everything flows through Org. Context is text. Responses are text. Diffs are text. This means standard Emacs operations—search, replace, version control, export—work on LLM interactions the same as any other buffer content.

*** Explicit Context
No implicit "send my whole project." The user declares what goes into the context window:
- =@handle= syntax resolves to specific Org nodes, files, or org-roam entries
- =ogent-codemap= generates a navigable index of the codebase
- =ogent-pin-dwim= persists items across requests
- =ogent-context-preview= shows exactly what will be sent

This explicitness serves two purposes: reproducibility (same input → same behavior) and efficiency (smaller context → faster responses, lower cost).

*** Responses as Data
Model output lands in Org src blocks with structured headers:
#+begin_example
#+begin_src text :model claude-sonnet-4-6 :status done :latency 2.1s
#+end_example

This metadata enables programmatic access. Fold responses, navigate between them, extract them for export. The response is not ephemeral chat—it's a first-class Org element.

*** Diffs Over Descriptions
When the model suggests code changes, ogent renders them as smerge conflicts:
- Red/green highlighting shows exactly what changed
- =C-c C-c= accepts, =C-c C-k= rejects
- No parsing prose like "change line 42 to..."

Visual review is faster than textual review. The interface should optimize for the bottleneck, which is human verification.

** Technical Implementation

*** Context Pipeline
1. =ogent-context-build= resolves the current subtree, ancestors, and =@handle= dependencies
2. =ogent-context-build-lazy= defers expensive resolution until needed
3. Context flows as an immutable plist—presentation code never mutates it
4. =ogent-response-function= fires exactly once per request for reliable hook execution

*** Model Orchestration
- =ogent-model-registry= declares backends with =:id=, =:backend=, =:stream?=, and optional =:preset=
- =ogent-prompt-dispatch= can fan out to multiple models simultaneously
- =ogent-ui--request-table= tracks concurrent streams for cancellation/retry
- gptel handles transport; ogent handles orchestration and presentation

*** Companion Buffers
When invoked from non-Org buffers, ogent creates a companion Org buffer for the transcript:
- Code buffer receives inline diffs/patches
- Companion buffer records prompts, context, and responses
- Markers keep the two synchronized
- Navigation commands work from either buffer

*** Tool Execution
- =ogent-tool-registry= defines available tools with approval workflows
- Tool results render in =#+begin_tool= blocks, folded by default
- =ogent-tool-fsm= manages the approval state machine
- Users can re-run tools at point with =ogent-tool-rerun=

*** Proof Ledger
Requests and tool calls may be recorded through =ogent-ledger.el= when
=ogent-ledger-enabled= is non-nil. Ledger entries are append-only Org
headings with event type, hash metadata, and printable event data.

The ledger is intentionally explicit:
- Request entries store prompt and context hashes, not full prompt payloads.
- Tool entries store declared effects, result hashes, errors, and duration.
- Buffer and marker values are sanitized to printable references.

This gives ogent a replayable audit trail without hidden memory.

*** Org Cabinet Layer
Cabinet-style knowledge-base and AI-team features live behind an Org storage
contract. The durable records are Org files, not JSON databases or Markdown
frontmatter:
- cabinet roots use =index.org= with =OGENT_CABINET= properties
- agents use =.agents/<slug>/persona.org=
- recurring jobs use =.agents/<slug>/jobs/<job-id>.org=
- conversations should use Org transcript files with the same src/tool block
  conventions as normal ogent requests
- =ogent-cabinet-build-graph= materializes those files into a typed directed
  graph with =cabinet=, =agent=, and =job= nodes plus semantic edges such as
  =contains= and =owns=
- =ogent-cabinet-status= renders that graph as the Cabinet operational entry
  point and links into =ogent-issues= and =ogent-gastown-status=
- =ogent-cabinet-runner= executes agents and jobs through local Codex or Claude
  CLI subscriptions, then persists each run as an Org transcript under the
  agent's session directory

See [[file:cabinet-org-os.org][Org Cabinet Integration]] for the full mapping from
Cabinet's repository architecture to ogent's Emacs/Org architecture.

*** Tool Effects
Every tool spec should declare =:effects=. Effects are plists with:
- =:kind= such as =read=, =write=, =execute=, =network=, =git=,
  =issue=, or =emacs-state=
- =:target= such as =file=, =filesystem=, =shell=, or =external=
- =:scope= such as =workspace=, =process=, =command=, or =unrestricted=
- =:risk= such as =low=, =medium=, =high=, or =critical=

Approval policy must consider effects, not only tool names. Read-only
workspace tools can run without prompting by default, while write,
execute, network, git, issue, and Emacs-state effects require approval.

* Rule of Engagement
- Treat this file as required context before building any feature.
- Emacs Lisp modules must stay under =lisp/=, UI helpers under =lisp/ui/=, docs under =docs/=, specs here.
- Every new command exported to users needs an =ogent-= prefix and an associated test in =test/= mirroring the namespace.

* Minor Mode Contract
- =ogent-mode= owns the =C-c o= prefix; do not bind global keys directly.
- Autoload interactive entrypoints so Doom packaging can lazily load.
- Keep state local to buffers: use buffer-local variables or plists on Org properties.

* Context Pipeline
1. Resolve the current subtree via =ogent-context-build=.
2. Collect ancestor headings, handles, and dependency plists.
3. Pass the plist unchanged into the UI layer; presentation code must not mutate nodes.
4. All model dispatchers must call =ogent-response-function= exactly once per request so hooks fire reliably.

* Codemap & Discovery
- Codemap output => Org subtree under a dedicated buffer to keep navigation consistent.
- When adding new namespaces, update =ogent-codemap-source-directories= and write tests proving definitions are discovered.

* Testing Expectations
- Use =ogent-test-with-fixture= when Org buffers are involved.
- For UI commands, assert both structural changes (e.g., src block insertion) and guard-rail behavior (model toggles, preview buffer creation).
- Always run =make test= and =make lint= before committing.

* Model Registry & Transport
- Declare every provider in =lisp/ogent-models.el=. Each entry must include =:id=, =:backend=, and =:stream?=. Optional keys (=:preset=, =:description=) feed the UI and docs.
- `ogent-prompt-dispatch` is generated from the registry. Never hard-code model buttons; call =ogent-ui-refresh-dispatch= after changing the registry so tests see the new toggle set.
- All transport code is expected to go through gptel (see [[file:gptel/overview.org][gptel overview]] and [[file:gptel-integration.org][integration plan]]). No direct HTTP clients inside ogent.
- Keep =ogent-model-registry= and =ogent-gptel-required-features= in sync so `ogent-ui--ensure-gptel` can `require` the right backend feature before streaming.

* Streaming & Error Handling
- `ogent-response-function` must return an =ogent-ui-request= struct. The UI layer is responsible for inserting placeholder Org blocks before gptel fires.
- Streaming callbacks append to the existing block and close it by writing =#+end_src= when gptel signals done/abort. Errors must produce a =#+begin_quote ogent-error= block without deleting prior context.
- Maintain the request table (=ogent-ui--request-table=) so cancellation/resume features can target active streams.
- Hooks (`ogent-after-request-hook`) are run exactly once per request—after blocks close successfully or with error annotations.

* Buffer Linking Outside Org-mode
- Invoking ogent from a non-Org major mode must establish (or reuse) a companion Org buffer that holds the request/response transcript. By default, create a temp Org buffer named after the source buffer (e.g., `*ogent:<file>*`) and store the link in buffer-local metadata so follow-up commands reuse the same companion.
- Users can override the companion by selecting an existing Org buffer (prompt or config). Once linked, ogent commands route context reads to the originating buffer and writes/streamed responses to the Org companion.
- All editing actions must respect the active context: code buffers receive inline diffs/patches when the user asks for edits, while the Org companion records prompts, context summaries, and streamed completions. Keep the two buffers synchronized via markers so navigation commands (e.g., jump to last response) work regardless of where ogent was invoked.
- Ensure the linking metadata survives buffer reloads (e.g., via buffer-local vars saved in file-local settings) and expose a command to rebind the companion Org buffer when users switch workflows.

* Proof Ledger & Effects
- =ogent-ledger.el= owns append-only request and tool event recording.
- =ogent-tool-effects.el= owns effect normalization, formatting, risk
  scoring, and approval policy primitives.
- Ledger recording is gated by =ogent-ledger-enabled=.
- New tools must declare =:effects= in their registry spec.
- Approval UI should display declared effects before arguments.
- Context manifests should include hashes and reasons for every included
  source, Org node, handle, and pinned item.

* Extending Specs
If a feature introduces new architectural rules, add a child heading here or create another file under =specs/= and cross-link it.

+  "Cabinet status dispatch keys remain active in Evil normal state."
+  (let ((ogent-cabinet-status-mode-hook nil)
+        states
+        maps)
+    (cl-letf (((symbol-function 'evil-set-initial-state)
+               (lambda (mode state)
+                 (push (cons mode state) states)))
+              ((symbol-function 'evil-make-overriding-map)
+               (lambda (map state)
+                 (push (cons map state) maps)))
+              ((symbol-function 'evil-normalize-keymaps)
+               (lambda (&rest _) nil)))
+      (ogent-cabinet-status--setup-evil))
+    (should (member (cons 'ogent-cabinet-status-mode 'normal) states))
+    (should (member (cons ogent-cabinet-status-mode-map 'all) maps))

## Cabinet Home

`M-x ogent-cabinet-home` is the Cabinet entry point. It opens a native Emacs dashboard backed by `index.org` and `.agents/**.org` records. The home view shows metadata, health counts, recent activity, failed work, stale jobs, missing persona fields, app artifacts, and navigation to the rest of the Cabinet.

Common commands:

| Key | Command |
|-----|---------|
| `RET` | Visit the item at point |
| `g` | Refresh |
| `q` | Quit |
| `a` | Agents |
| `t` | Tasks |
| `c` | Conversations |
| `s` | Search |
| `A` | Apps |
| `G` | Graph/status |
| `e` | Edit Cabinet metadata |
| `n` / `p` | Move between actionable rows |

The main ogent dispatch bindings include:

| Key | Command |
|-----|---------|
| `C-c . j` / `SPC o j` | `ogent-cabinet-home` |
| `C-c . K` / `SPC o K` | `ogent-cabinet-status` |
| `C-c . y` / `SPC o y` | `ogent-cabinet-agents` |
| `C-c . Y` / `SPC o Y` | `ogent-cabinet-agent` |
| `C-c . I` / `SPC o I` | `ogent-cabinet-tasks` |
| `C-c . O` / `SPC o O` | `ogent-cabinet-conversations` |
| `C-c . V` / `SPC o V` | `ogent-cabinet-search` |
| `C-c . W` / `SPC o W` | `ogent-cabinet-apps` |
| `C-c . X` / `SPC o X` | `ogent-cabinet-create-agent` |
| `C-c . Z` / `SPC o Z` | `ogent-cabinet-create-job` |

See [docs/cabinet.org](docs/cabinet.org) for the first-ten-minutes workflow and import limits.

## AI & Knowledge Sources
- **LLM backend**: ogent leans on `gptel`'s transport layer for streaming completions, credentials, and model selection.
- **Graph awareness**: Inspired by `org-roam`, ogent can query a local Org-roam database to resolve `@handle`s across files, making long-lived knowledge bases available to every buffer.

## gptel Integration Status
- Dynamic dispatcher buttons are generated from `ogent-models.el`, so contributors can define additional providers without editing UI code.
- `ogent-request` streams responses chunk-by-chunk through gptel callbacks, inserting placeholder `#+begin_src` blocks and closing them when completions finish or error.
- Specs live under `specs/gptel/` (`overview.org`, `gptel-integration.org`) and describe how we bridge presets, backends, and streaming hooks. Read them before adjusting transport behavior.
- `ogent-ui--ensure-gptel` auto-loads every feature listed in `ogent-gptel-required-features`, so when you add a provider extend both the registry entry and that defcustom to guarantee the backend structs exist before dispatch.
- FSM status tracking is implemented via `ogent-tool-fsm.el`, with visual state indicators in the mode line.
- Tool-call rendering is handled by `ogent-tool-render.el`, displaying reasoning and tool blocks inline.
- Backend/preset configuration is documented in [docs/backends-and-presets.md](docs/backends-and-presets.md) and the `ogent-onboard` wizard.
- Workspace presets allow per-project model and backend configuration via `.ogent-presets`.

## Backends, Models, and Presets
- `docs/backends-and-presets.md` walks through backend switching (gptel backend selection), model registry configuration, preset definition, and troubleshooting.
- Use the prompt dispatcher (`C-c . p`, or `SPC o p` in Doom/Evil) to pick a provider/model (`m`), apply a preset (`s`), or fan out across multiple models (`M`).

## Module Overview

ogent is organized into focused modules under `lisp/`:

| Module | Purpose |
|--------|---------|
| `ogent.el`, `ogent-core.el` | Entry points and core infrastructure |
| `ogent-keys.el` | Keybinding management |
| `ogent-models.el`, `ogent-presets.el` | Model registry and preset configuration |
| `ogent-context.el` | Context building from Org hierarchies |
| `ogent-prompts.el`, `ogent-prompts-yasnippet.el` | Prompt templates and snippet integration |
| `ogent-codemap.el` | Repository analysis and codemap generation |
| `ogent-completions.el`, `ogent-session.el` | Completion handling and session buffers |
| `ogent-edit*.el`, `inline-diff.el` | AI-powered code editing (diff, display, format, parse, word-level inline diff) |
| `ogent-tool*.el` | Tool system (approval, FSM, rendering) |
| `ogent-cabinet*.el`, `ui/ogent-ui-cabinet.el` | Org-native Cabinet storage, CLI runner, graph status, agents, profiles, tasks, search, and app opening |
| `ogent-issues*.el` | Beads issue tracker integration |
| `ogent-gastown*.el`, `ogent-refinery.el` | Gas Town multi-agent coordination |
| `ogent-onboard.el`, `ogent-anthropic-oauth.el` | Setup wizard and OAuth |
| `ogent-debug.el`, `ogent-mcp.el` | Debugging and MCP integration |

## Recent Additions

The following features were added recently:

- **Request Pause/Resume** (`ogent-ui.el`): Pause active requests and resume later with full context preservation. Commands `ogent-pause-request` and `ogent-resume-request`.
- **Tool Result Streaming** (`ogent-tools.el`): Async tool execution with streaming callbacks for bash, grep, and other long-running operations. Supports `:stream` and `:match` callback styles.
- **Inline Diff Display** (`inline-diff.el`): Word-level inline diff highlighting as an alternative to smerge. Toggle with `ogent-edit-toggle-display-method` (cycles smerge → overlay → inline-diff).
- **Beads Integration** (`ogent-issues.el`): Magit-style buffer for browsing and managing beads issues with inline filtering, transient menus, and dependency graph visualization.
- **Gas Town Multi-Agent** (`ogent-gastown.el`): Status buffer and tmux integration for coordinating multiple AI agent workspaces.
- **Org Cabinet Foundation and Rich UI** (`ogent-cabinet.el`, `ogent-cabinet-runner.el`, `ogent-cabinet-status.el`, `ui/ogent-ui-cabinet.el`): Org-backed Cabinet roots, agents, jobs, CLI-backed Codex/Claude runs, saved Org transcripts, graph status with Issues/Gas Town bridges, agent profile buffers, attention lanes, search, and app artifact opening.
- **Refinery Buffer** (`ogent-refinery.el`): Merge queue visualization for tracking and managing pending merges.
- **Session Management** (`ogent-session.el`): Improved Org hierarchy with proper request/response threading and inline prompting.
- **Tool System** (`ogent-tool-*.el`): Complete tool approval UI, FSM status tracking, and inline rendering of tool calls/results.
- **Onboarding Wizard** (`ogent-onboard.el`): Interactive setup for API keys and provider configuration with OAuth support.
- **Default Prompts** (`ogent-prompts.el`): Reusable prompt templates with yasnippet integration.
- **Code Editing** (`ogent-edit.el`): AI-powered code editing with diff preview and apply/reject workflow.

## Roadmap

### Completed
- ✓ Tool result streaming with async callbacks
- ✓ Request pause/resume capability
- ✓ Inline-diff word-level display alternative
- ✓ Multi-model fan-out and comparison
- ✓ MCP server integration
- ✓ Magit-style diff preview UX

### In Progress
- **Incremental Codemap Refresh**: Detect changed files and update only affected sections while preserving manual annotations.
- **Prompt Template Library**: Expand built-in templates for code review, refactoring, documentation, and debugging workflows.

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba specs/architecture.org | sed -n '70,120p'" in /Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent
 succeeded in 0ms:
    70	- Request entries store prompt and context hashes, not full prompt payloads.
    71	- Tool entries store declared effects, result hashes, errors, and duration.
    72	- Buffer and marker values are sanitized to printable references.
    73
    74	This gives ogent a replayable audit trail without hidden memory.
    75
    76	*** Org Cabinet Layer
    77	Cabinet-style knowledge-base and AI-team features live behind an Org storage
    78	contract. The durable records are Org files, not JSON databases or Markdown
    79	frontmatter:
    80	- cabinet roots use =index.org= with =OGENT_CABINET= properties
    81	- agents use =.agents/<slug>/persona.org=
    82	- recurring jobs use =.agents/<slug>/jobs/<job-id>.org=
    83	- conversations should use Org transcript files with the same src/tool block
    84	  conventions as normal ogent requests
    85	- =ogent-cabinet-build-graph= materializes those files into a typed directed
    86	  graph with =cabinet=, =agent=, and =job= nodes plus semantic edges such as
    87	  =contains= and =owns=
    88	- =ogent-cabinet-status= renders that graph as the Cabinet operational entry
    89	  point and links into =ogent-issues= and =ogent-gastown-status=
    90	- =ogent-cabinet-runner= executes agents and jobs through local Codex or Claude
    91	  CLI subscriptions, then persists each run as an Org transcript under the
    92	  agent's session directory
    93
    94	See [[file:cabinet-org-os.org][Org Cabinet Integration]] for the full mapping from
    95	Cabinet's repository architecture to ogent's Emacs/Org architecture.
    96
    97	*** Tool Effects
    98	Every tool spec should declare =:effects=. Effects are plists with:
    99	- =:kind= such as =read=, =write=, =execute=, =network=, =git=,
   100	  =issue=, or =emacs-state=
   101	- =:target= such as =file=, =filesystem=, =shell=, or =external=
   102	- =:scope= such as =workspace=, =process=, =command=, or =unrestricted=
   103	- =:risk= such as =low=, =medium=, =high=, or =critical=
   104
   105	Approval policy must consider effects, not only tool names. Read-only
   106	workspace tools can run without prompting by default, while write,
   107	execute, network, git, issue, and Emacs-state effects require approval.
   108
   109	* Rule of Engagement
   110	- Treat this file as required context before building any feature.
   111	- Emacs Lisp modules must stay under =lisp/=, UI helpers under =lisp/ui/=, docs under =docs/=, specs here.
   112	- Every new command exported to users needs an =ogent-= prefix and an associated test in =test/= mirroring the namespace.
   113
   114	* Minor Mode Contract
   115	- =ogent-mode= owns the =C-c o= prefix; do not bind global keys directly.
   116	- Autoload interactive entrypoints so Doom packaging can lazily load.
   117	- Keep state local to buffers: use buffer-local variables or plists on Org properties.
   118
   119	* Context Pipeline
   120	1. Resolve the current subtree via =ogent-context-build=.

     1	#+title: Cabinet User Guide
     2
     3	* What Cabinet Is
     4
     5	Cabinet is an Org-backed local knowledge OS for AI-team work inside Emacs. A
     6	Cabinet root is a directory with =index.org= plus agent, job, conversation,
     7	task, app, import, and relationship records stored as Org files.
     8
     9	The main command is =M-x ogent-cabinet-home=. It opens a single operational UI
    10	with metadata, health counts, navigation, recent activity, and work needing
    11	attention. Failed work is shown in Cabinet Home and on the task board.
    12
    13	* Durable Layout
    14
    15	#+begin_example
    16	cabinet-root/
    17	  index.org
    18	  imports/
    19	  .agents/
    20	    editor/
    21	      persona.org
    22	      inbox.org
    23	      schedule.org
    24	      jobs/
    25	        weekly-review.org
    26	      memory/
    27	        context.org
    28	        decisions.org
    29	        learnings.org
    30	      sessions/
    31	        20260504T090000-weekly-review.org
    32	#+end_example
    33
    34	Org is the durable source of truth. Commands edit property drawers and body
    35	text in those Org files. Manual edits remain part of the record.
    36
    37	* First 10 Minutes
    38
    39	1. Create a Cabinet:
    40
    41	   #+begin_src emacs-lisp
    42	   (ogent-cabinet-scaffold "~/cabinet/acme" "Acme Cabinet" :kind "root")
    43	   #+end_src
    44
    45	2. Open the operating surface:
    46
    47	   #+begin_example
    48	   M-x ogent-cabinet-home
    49	   #+end_example
    50
    51	3. Create an agent:
    52
    53	   #+begin_example
    54	   M-x ogent-cabinet-create-agent
    55	   #+end_example
    56
    57	   Fill in name, slug, role, provider, model, workspace, tags, and persona.
    58
    59	4. Add a recurring job:
    60
    61	   #+begin_example
    62	   M-x ogent-cabinet-create-job
    63	   #+end_example
    64
    65	   The job is written under =.agents/<slug>/jobs/<job-id>.org=.
    66
    67	5. Run the job:
    68
    69	   Open =M-x ogent-cabinet-jobs=, move to the job, press =R=.
    70
    71	6. Inspect the transcript:
    72
    73	   Open =M-x ogent-cabinet-conversations= and press =RET= on the new run.
    74	   The detail buffer shows metadata, prompt, output, tool blocks, errors,
    75	   app links, duration, and source Org.
    76
    77	7. Search the Cabinet:
    78
    79	   Use =M-x ogent-cabinet-search=. Empty queries show an empty state. Search
    80	   can filter by kind, agent, status, tag, and archive state from Lisp callers.
    81
    82	8. Open generated apps:
    83
    84	   Use =M-x ogent-cabinet-apps=. Each =index.html= below the Cabinet root is
    85	   listed with label, path, modified time, and inferred owner when possible.
    86
    87	9. Check the task board:
    88
    89	   Use =M-x ogent-cabinet-tasks=. Lanes are Inbox, Needs Reply, Running,
    90	   Scheduled, Just Finished, Stale, and Archive.
    91
    92	10. Inspect relationships:
    93
    94	    Use =M-x ogent-cabinet-status=. The graph includes cabinet, agent, job,
    95	    session, app, issue-link, and Gas Town hook nodes when available.
    96
    97	* Keybindings

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba README.md | sed -n '15,110p'" in /Users/jake/vault/projects/ogent
 succeeded in 0ms:
    15	- **Context scoping**: Invoking `M-x ogent-request` collects the current heading, all ancestor headings, and any `@handle` dependencies into a structured payload. Handles can point to other buffers or Org-roam files, so the request can include folders that “fill out” missing knowledge while still rooting the prompt in the active subtree.
    16	- **Context preview**: Before dispatching, ogent renders the same hydrated payload it will send to the model, including the root subtree, resolved `@handle` content, source buffer or region, and pins.
    17	- **Prompt templates**: Users can store reusable AI instructions inside dedicated “Prompt” subtrees. Because they are just Org nodes, the same `@handle` syntax applies.
    18	- **Native Agent**: Each buffer acts as both the chat surface and the canonical plan—responses appear inline, can be edited like any Org node, and remain linked to their source prompts so the evolving document stays in sync with agent output. This is the most important concept of `ogent` - it should act as a homunculus that can be instantiated at any point in your Emacs workflow.
    19	- **Codemaps**: ogent can scan the repository (or referenced folders) to synthesize “codemaps” that resemble Windsurf’s maps. Each codemap is an Org subtree listing modules, entry points, and data flows with bullet links back to files (e.g., `[[file:lisp/ogent-context.el::ogent-context-build][context builder]]`). Use `C-c . m` to refresh the map so contributors always see a high-level architecture next to the agent transcript.
    20	- **Model registry**: `lisp/ogent-models.el` lists every supported gptel backend (id, preset, stream support). The dispatcher and transport stack look up this registry so adding a provider is a data change plus tests, not a UI surgery.
    21	- **Org Cabinet OS**: `ogent-cabinet-scaffold` creates Cabinet-style knowledge bases as Org files, then `ogent-cabinet-home` (`C-c . j`, `SPC o j`) opens the operational home view. From there a user can manage agents, jobs, tasks, conversations, search, generated app artifacts, and the graph/status projection. All durable records stay in Org, including personas, jobs, transcripts, imports, and metadata edits.
    22
    23	## Prompt Capture & Formatting
    24	- **Command palette**: `C-c . p` (`ogent-prompt-dispatch`) opens a transient that lets you pick one or more models, select prompt templates, and send the current subtree context with a single keystroke. Doom/Evil users get the same surface under `SPC o`.
    25	- **AI speed edit**: `C-c . v` (`SPC o v` in Doom/Evil) lets the model choose the highest-value small edit from the active selection, point context, and editor diagnostics, then routes the patch through the inline review flow.
    26	- **Diagnostic repair**: `C-c . f` (`SPC o f` in Doom/Evil) grabs the Flymake or Flycheck diagnostic at point, builds a focused repair prompt, and applies the result through the inline edit review flow.
    27	- **Buffer diagnostic sweep**: `C-c . F` (`SPC o F` in Doom/Evil) ranks every Flymake or Flycheck diagnostic in the current buffer and requests one reviewable repair patch.
    28	- **Quick inline edit**: `C-c . k` (`SPC o k` in Doom/Evil) prompts for one instruction and targets the active region, current definition, or current line. Use a prefix argument for full-file edits.
    29	- **Src block insertion**: Immediate completions land inside a language-aware `#+begin_src` block (`ogent-src-backend`). Hit `C-c C-c` to execute or reify the block directly in place.
    30	- **Notes capture**: Press `C-c C-d` on a completion snippet to shunt it beneath the current subtree inside a collapsed `Notes` headline, keeping speculative ideas separate from canonical content.
    31	- **Multi-model fan-out**: Selecting multiple providers triggers concurrent gptel requests via the registry; each response streams into its own src block tagged with model/backend metadata so you can compare answers side-by-side without blocking.
    32	- **Ergonomic review**: `C-c o n` / `C-c o p` cycle through completions, `C-c o a` accepts the current one (deleting others), and `C-c o x` rejects it. Visual feedback dims non-current completions and optionally folds them.
    33	- **Context hydration**: The dispatcher resolves referenced `@handles`, includes their content in the model payload, and offers a `C-c . c` preview of that payload before dispatch.
    34
    35	## Codemap Overview
    36	- `M-x ogent-codemap-buffer` (bound to `C-c . m`) analyzes the repository or selected folders, extracts public definitions, and emits an Org subtree titled “Codemap”. Each entry includes inline links such as `[[file:lisp/ogent-context.el::ogent-context-build][Context Builder]]` so you can jump straight to the code.
    37	- Codemaps update incrementally: rerun the command to refresh sections impacted by recent changes while preserving manual annotations.
    38	- The codemap subtree doubles as a navigational aid and a prompt attachment—mark it with an `OGENT_ID` (`OGENT_ID: codemap-core`) and reference it via `@codemap-core` whenever you want the model to understand the project layout.
    39	- Inspired by Windsurf’s codemaps, ogent surfaces data-flow descriptions (“`ogent-prompt-dispatch -> ogent-context-build -> gptel-send`”) directly under each bullet, so the map reads like an architecture digest next to your agent transcript.
    40
    41	## Planned Workflow
    42	1. Author Org content as usual, tagging reusable sections with unique `OGENT_ID`s.
    43	2. Reference needed sections inline (`The overview lives in @overview-block`) to shape the context hierarchy.
    44	3. Run `M-x ogent-request` (or `C-c . p`) to send the current tree plus referenced blocks, and any attached external documents, to the selected model(s) via `gptel`, reviewing the hydrated payload before dispatch.
    45	4. Evaluate each src block (`C-c C-c`) or archive it as a `Notes` child (`C-c C-d`), then promote accepted knowledge into the permanent subtree structure.
    46
    47	## Doom Emacs
    48
    49	For Doom Emacs users, ogent provides an idiomatic configuration with keybindings under `SPC o`. See the full guide at [docs/doom-emacs.md](docs/doom-emacs.md).
    50
    51	**Quick start** - add to `~/.doom.d/packages.el`:
    52
    53	```elisp
    54	(package! ogent :recipe (:local-repo "~/path/to/ogent/lisp"
    55	                         :files ("*.el" "ui/*.el")))
    56	```
    57
    58	Then run `doom sync` and add this to `~/.doom.d/config.el`:
    59
    60	```elisp
    61	(use-package! ogent
    62	  :defer t
    63	  :commands (ogent-mode ogent-prompt-dispatch ogent-request
    64	             ogent-ai-speed-edit)
    65	  :init
    66	  (setq ogent-enable-doom-bindings t
    67	        ogent-doom-prefix "o")
    68	  :config
    69	  (ogent-setup-doom-bindings)
    70	  (ogent-global-mode 1))
    71	```

   989	(defun ogent-cabinet-clone-agent (&optional directory agent-slug new-slug)
   990	  "Clone AGENT-SLUG under DIRECTORY to NEW-SLUG."
   991	  (interactive
   992	   (let* ((root (ogent-cabinet-ui--root
   993	                 (or (ogent-cabinet-find-root)
   994	                     (read-directory-name "Cabinet root: "))))
   995	          (slug (ogent-cabinet-ui--read-agent root)))
   996	     (list root slug (read-string "New slug: " (concat slug "-copy")))))
   997	  (let* ((root (ogent-cabinet-ui--root directory))
   998	         (agent (copy-sequence (ogent-cabinet-read-agent root agent-slug)))
   999	         (target (or new-slug (read-string "New slug: " (concat agent-slug "-copy")))))
  1000	    (when (file-exists-p (ogent-cabinet-agent-file root target))
  1001	      (user-error "Agent already exists: %s" target))
  1002	    (plist-put agent :slug target)
  1003	    (plist-put agent :name (format "%s Copy" (or (plist-get agent :name)
  1004	                                                 agent-slug)))
  1005	    (plist-put agent :active t)
  1006	    (plist-put agent :archived nil)
  1007	    (ogent-cabinet-write-agent root agent (plist-get agent :body))))
  1008

  1014	                 (or (ogent-cabinet-find-root)
  1015	                     (read-directory-name "Cabinet root: "))))
  1016	          (slug (ogent-cabinet-ui--read-agent root)))

  1042	  (setq-local tabulated-list-format

  1056	(defun ogent-cabinet-job-next-run (job)
  1057	  "Return a friendly next-run description for JOB."
  1058	  (cond
  1059	   ((plist-get job :archived) "archived")
  1060	   ((not (plist-get job :enabled)) "disabled")
  1061	   ((ogent-cabinet--blank-to-nil (plist-get job :cron))
  1062	    (format "cron %s" (plist-get job :cron)))
  1063	   ((ogent-cabinet--blank-to-nil (plist-get job :heartbeat))
  1064	    (format "heartbeat %s" (plist-get job :heartbeat)))
  1065	   (t "manual")))
  1066
  1067	(defun ogent-cabinet-jobs--entry (job)
  1068	  "Return a tabulated entry for JOB."
  1069	  (let* ((agent (plist-get job :agent))
  1070	         (job-id (plist-get job :id))
  1071	         (file (ogent-cabinet-job-file ogent-cabinet-jobs--root agent job-id)))
  1072	    (list
  1073	     (append (list :type 'job :path file :agent agent :job-id job-id) job)
  1074	     (vector
  1075	      agent
  1076	      (format "%s (%s)" (or (plist-get job :name) job-id) job-id)
  1077	      (if (plist-get job :enabled) "yes" "no")
  1078	      (ogent-cabinet-job-next-run job)
  1079	      (or (plist-get job :provider) "")
  1080	      (or (plist-get job :model) "")
  1081	      (or (plist-get job :workspace) "")
  1082	      (ogent-cabinet-ui--format-tags (plist-get job :tags))))))

  1088	                                      ogent-cabinet-jobs--agent)))

   843	  "Return a graph node plist for ID, KIND, LABEL, PATH, and DATA."

   850	(defun ogent-cabinet--graph-edge (from to kind &optional data)
   851	  "Return a graph edge plist from FROM to TO with KIND and DATA."
   852	  (let ((edge (list :from from :to to :kind kind)))
   853	    (if data
   854	        (plist-put edge :data data)

   857	(defun ogent-cabinet--issue-links (root)
   858	  "Return Org records under ROOT with issue link metadata."
   859	  (let (links)
   860	    (dolist (file (ogent-cabinet-org-files root))
   861	      (let ((metadata (ogent-cabinet-record-metadata file)))
   862	        (when (plist-get metadata :issue-id)
   863	          (push (append (list :path file) metadata) links))))
   864	    (nreverse links)))

   878	(defun ogent-cabinet-build-graph (directory)
   879	  "Return a typed graph projection for the Org cabinet under DIRECTORY.
   880	The returned plist has `:nodes' and `:edges' collections suitable for
   881	status buffers, future incremental indexes, and automation planners."
   882	  (let* ((candidate (ogent-cabinet--directory directory))
   883	         (root (file-truename
   884	                (ogent-cabinet--directory
   885	                 (or (ogent-cabinet-find-root candidate)
   886	                     candidate))))
   887	         (index (ogent-cabinet-read-index root))
   888	         (cabinet-id "cabinet:.")
   889	         (nodes (list (ogent-cabinet--graph-node
   890	                       cabinet-id
   891	                       'cabinet
   892	                       (plist-get index :name)
   893	                       (plist-get index :path)
   894	                       index)))
   895	         (edges nil))
   896	    (dolist (slug (ogent-cabinet-list-agents root))
   897	      (let* ((agent (ogent-cabinet-read-agent root slug))
   898	             (agent-id (format "agent:%s" slug)))
   899	        (push (ogent-cabinet--graph-node
   900	               agent-id
   901	               'agent
   902	               (or (plist-get agent :name) slug)
   903	               (ogent-cabinet-agent-file root slug)
   904	               agent)
   905	              nodes)
   906	        (push (ogent-cabinet--graph-edge cabinet-id agent-id 'contains)
   907	              edges)
   908	        (dolist (job (ogent-cabinet-list-jobs root slug))
   909	          (let* ((job-id (plist-get job :id))
   910	                 (node-id (format "job:%s/%s" slug job-id)))
   911	            (push (ogent-cabinet--graph-node
   912	                   node-id
   913	                   'job
   914	                   (or (plist-get job :name) job-id)
   915	                   (ogent-cabinet-job-file root slug job-id)
   916	                   job)
   917	                  nodes)
   918	            (push (ogent-cabinet--graph-edge agent-id node-id 'owns)
   919	                  edges)
   920	            (push (ogent-cabinet--graph-edge node-id agent-id 'scheduled-by)
   921	                  edges)))
   922	        (dolist (session (ogent-cabinet-list-sessions root slug))
   923	          (let* ((session-id (plist-get session :id))
   924	                 (node-id (format "session:%s/%s" slug session-id))
   925	                 (job-id (plist-get session :job-id)))
   926	            (push (ogent-cabinet--graph-node
   927	                   node-id
   928	                   'session
   929	                   (or (plist-get session :name) session-id)
   930	                   (plist-get session :path)
   931	                   session)
   932	                  nodes)
   933	            (push (ogent-cabinet--graph-edge agent-id node-id 'produced)
   934	                  edges)
   935	            (when (plist-get session :archived)
   936	              (push (ogent-cabinet--graph-edge cabinet-id node-id 'archived-from)
   937	                    edges))
   938	            (when (and job-id (not (string-empty-p job-id)))
   939	              (push (ogent-cabinet--graph-edge
   940	                     (format "job:%s/%s" slug job-id)
   941	                     node-id
   942	                     (if (equal (plist-get session :status) "FAILED")
   943	                         'failed-from
   944	                       'produced))
   945	                    edges))))))
   946	    (dolist (app (ogent-cabinet-list-apps root))
   947	      (let* ((label (plist-get app :label))
   948	             (node-id (format "app:%s" label)))
   949	        (push (ogent-cabinet--graph-node
   950	               node-id
   951	               'app
   952	               label
   953	               (plist-get app :path)
   954	               app)
   955	              nodes)
   956	        (push (ogent-cabinet--graph-edge cabinet-id node-id 'contains)
   957	              edges)
   958	        (when-let ((session-id (plist-get app :session-id)))
   959	          (let ((session-node (format "session:%s/%s"
   960	                                      (plist-get app :agent)
   961	                                      session-id)))
   962	            (push (ogent-cabinet--graph-edge session-node node-id 'produced)
   963	                  edges)))))
   964	    (dolist (issue (ogent-cabinet--issue-links root))
   965	      (let* ((issue-id (plist-get issue :issue-id))
   966	             (node-id (format "issue:%s" issue-id))

   972	               (plist-get issue :path)

   974	              nodes)

   976	              edges)
   977	        (when worker
   978	          (push (ogent-cabinet--graph-edge node-id
   979	                                           (format "agent:%s" worker)
   980	                                           'assigned-worker)

   222	  "Insert graph summary section."
   223	  (let* ((cabinet (car (ogent-cabinet-status--nodes-by-kind 'cabinet)))
   224	         (nodes (plist-get ogent-cabinet-status--graph :nodes))
   225	         (edges (plist-get ogent-cabinet-status--graph :edges)))

   228	      (ogent-cabinet-status--insert-node-line

   231	               (propertize (or (plist-get cabinet :label) "Cabinet")
   232	                           'face 'ogent-cabinet-status-label)
   233	               (length nodes)
   234	               (length edges))))
   235	    (insert "  ")
   236	    (insert (propertize "Projection: " 'face 'ogent-cabinet-status-dimmed))
   237	    (insert "Org files -> typed graph -> operational views\n")))

   255	                            (plist-get data :slug))
   256	                           'working)
   257	                          ((plist-get data :active) 'active)

   260	             agent
   261	             (format "%s %s  %s  %s  %s"
   262	                     (propertize (ogent-ops-activity-symbol status)
   263	                                 'face (if (memq status '(active working))
   264	                                           'ogent-cabinet-status-connected
   265	                                         'ogent-cabinet-status-disconnected))

   267	                                 'face 'ogent-cabinet-status-label)

   271	                     (propertize provider

   275	                      'face 'ogent-cabinet-status-dimmed)))

   280	                 (ogent-cabinet-status--format-job-line job)

   301	                               'face 'ogent-cabinet-status-label))))

   333	  "Insert TEXT for NODE with optional PREFIX and visit metadata."

   448	          (plist-get data :agent)
   449	          (read-string "Instruction: "))))

     1	;;; ogent-cabinet.el --- Org-native cabinet storage -*- lexical-binding: t; -*-
     2
     3	;;; Commentary:
     4	;; Provides the file-backed storage foundation for Cabinet-style knowledge
     5	;; bases using Org files as the source of truth.
     6
     7	;;; Code:
     8
     9	(require 'cl-lib)
    10	(require 'org)
    11	(require 'seq)
    12	(require 'subr-x)
    13
    14	(defgroup ogent-cabinet nil
    15	  "Org-native Cabinet-style knowledge bases."
    16	  :group 'ogent)
    17
    18	(defcustom ogent-cabinet-default-agent-provider "codex"

    20	  :type 'string
    21	  :group 'ogent-cabinet)

    35	(defun ogent-cabinet--directory (directory)
    36	  "Return DIRECTORY as an expanded directory path."
    37	  (file-name-as-directory (expand-file-name directory)))
    38
    39	(defun ogent-cabinet--slug (value &optional fallback)
    40	  "Return VALUE normalized as a filesystem-safe slug.
    41	Use FALLBACK when VALUE normalizes to the empty string."
    42	  (let* ((base (downcase (string-trim (format "%s" (or value "")))))
    43	         (spaced (replace-regexp-in-string "[[:space:]]+" "-" base))
    44	         (clean (replace-regexp-in-string "[^[:alnum:]-]" "" spaced)))
    45	    (if (string-empty-p clean)
    46	        (or fallback "item")
    47	      clean)))
    48
    49	(defun ogent-cabinet--truth-value (value)
    50	  "Return t when VALUE represents true."
    51	  (cond
    52	   ((eq value t) t)
    53	   ((null value) nil)
    54	   ((stringp value)
    55	    (not (null (member (downcase (string-trim value))
    56		                       '("t" "true" "yes" "1")))))
    57	   (t nil)))
    58
    59	(defun ogent-cabinet--boolean-property-valid-p (value)
    60	  "Return non-nil when VALUE is blank or a known boolean string."
    61	  (or (null value)
    62	      (string-blank-p value)
    63	      (member (downcase (string-trim value))
    64	              '("t" "true" "yes" "1" "nil" "false" "no" "0"))))
    65
    66	(defun ogent-cabinet--cron-expression-p (value)
    67	  "Return non-nil when VALUE looks like a five-field cron expression."
    68	  (let ((parts (split-string (string-trim (or value "")) "[ \t]+" t)))
    69	    (= (length parts) 5)))
    70
    71	(defun ogent-cabinet--heartbeat-expression-p (value)
    72	  "Return non-nil when VALUE looks like a heartbeat or cron expression."
    73	  (let ((trimmed (string-trim (or value ""))))
    74	    (or (string-match-p "\\`[0-9]+[smhdw]?\\'" trimmed)
    75	        (ogent-cabinet--cron-expression-p trimmed))))
    76
    77	(defun ogent-cabinet--property-value (value)
    78	  "Return VALUE formatted for an Org property drawer."
    79	  (cond
    80	   ((eq value t) "t")
    81	   ((null value) "")
    82	   ((listp value)
    83	    (string-join (mapcar (lambda (item) (format "%s" item)) value) ", "))
    84	   (t (format "%s" value))))
    85
    86	(defun ogent-cabinet--format-properties (properties)
    87	  "Return PROPERTIES as an Org property drawer.
    88	PROPERTIES is an alist of property names to values."
    89	  (concat
    90	   ":PROPERTIES:\n"
    91	   (mapconcat
    92	    (lambda (property)
    93	      (format ":%s: %s"
    94	              (car property)
    95	              (ogent-cabinet--property-value (cdr property))))
    96	    properties
    97	    "\n")
    98	   "\n:END:\n"))
    99
   100	(defun ogent-cabinet--write-file (file content)
   101	  "Write CONTENT to FILE, creating parent directories first."
   102	  (make-directory (file-name-directory file) t)
   103	  (with-temp-file file
   104	    (insert content)))

   107	  "Write CONTENT to FILE when FILE does not exist."
   108	  (unless (file-exists-p file)
   109	    (ogent-cabinet--write-file file content)))

   112	  "Return tags parsed from VALUE."
   113	  (if (string-blank-p (or value ""))
   114	      nil
   115	    (split-string value "[ \t]*,[ \t]*" t)))
   116
   117	(defun ogent-cabinet--blank-to-nil (value)
   118	  "Return nil when VALUE is nil or blank."
   119	  (when (and value (not (string-blank-p value)))
   120	    value))

   122	(defun ogent-cabinet--heading-body ()
   123	  "Return the body text under the current Org heading."
   124	  (save-excursion
   125	    (org-back-to-heading t)
   126	    (org-end-of-meta-data t)
   127	    (let ((begin (point))
   128	          (end (save-excursion
   129	                 (org-end-of-subtree t t)
   130	                 (point))))
   131	      (string-trim (buffer-substring-no-properties begin end)))))

   134	  "Return the title of the first Org heading in the current buffer."
   135	  (goto-char (point-min))
   136	  (unless (re-search-forward org-heading-regexp nil t)
   137	    (user-error "No Org heading found"))
   138	  (org-back-to-heading t)
   139	  (nth 4 (org-heading-components)))

   197	(defun ogent-cabinet-root-p (directory)
   198	  "Return non-nil when DIRECTORY has an Org cabinet index."
   199	  (let ((index (ogent-cabinet-index-file directory)))
   200	    (and (file-exists-p index)
   201	         (with-temp-buffer
   202	           (insert-file-contents index nil 0 4096)
   203	           (goto-char (point-min))
   204	           (re-search-forward "^[ \t]*:OGENT_CABINET:[ \t]+t[ \t]*$" nil t)))))
   205
   206	(defun ogent-cabinet-find-root (&optional start)
   207	  "Return the nearest cabinet root at or above START.
   208	START defaults to `default-directory'."
   209	  (let ((dir (ogent-cabinet--directory (or start default-directory)))
   210	        (found nil)
   211	        parent)
   212	    (while (and dir (not found))
   213	      (if (ogent-cabinet-root-p dir)
   214	          (setq found dir)
   215	        (setq parent (file-name-directory (directory-file-name dir)))
   216	        (setq dir (unless (or (null parent) (equal parent dir))
   217	                    parent))))
   218	    (when found
   219	      (directory-file-name found))))

   258	;;;###autoload
   259	(cl-defun ogent-cabinet-scaffold
   260	    (directory name &key (kind "root") description body tags create-editor skip-existing)
   261	  "Create an Org-native cabinet named NAME in DIRECTORY.
   262	When CREATE-EDITOR is non-nil, also create the built-in editor agent.
   263	When SKIP-EXISTING is non-nil, keep an existing index file."
   264	  (interactive
   265	   (list (read-directory-name "Cabinet directory: ")
   266	         (read-string "Cabinet name: ")))
   267	  (let* ((root (ogent-cabinet--directory directory))
   268	         (index (ogent-cabinet-index-file root)))
   269	    (make-directory root t)
   270	    (dolist (relative ogent-cabinet--managed-directories)
   271	      (make-directory (expand-file-name relative root) t))
   272	    (if (and skip-existing (file-exists-p index))
   273	        index
   274	      (ogent-cabinet--write-file
   275	       index
   276	       (ogent-cabinet--format-index name kind description body tags)))
   277	    (when create-editor
   278	      (ogent-cabinet-write-agent
   279	       root
   280	       `(:slug "editor"
   281	         :name "Editor"
   282	         :role "Knowledge base editor"
   283	         :provider ,ogent-cabinet-default-agent-provider
   284	         :heartbeat ,ogent-cabinet-default-heartbeat
   285	         :active t
   286	         :workspace "/"
   287	         :tags ("editor" "knowledge"))
   288	       "Maintain Org pages, links, summaries, and agent-facing context."))
   289	    root))

   314	(defun ogent-cabinet--format-agent (agent body)
   315	  "Return AGENT and BODY formatted as an Org persona."

   317	                (ogent-cabinet--agent-plist-value agent :slug nil)
   318	                "agent"))
   319	         (name (ogent-cabinet--agent-plist-value agent :name slug))

   322	                    agent :provider ogent-cabinet-default-agent-provider))
   323	         (model (ogent-cabinet--agent-plist-value agent :model nil))
   324	         (permission-mode (ogent-cabinet--agent-plist-value
   325	                           agent :permission-mode nil))
   326	         (heartbeat (ogent-cabinet--agent-plist-value

   328	         (active (ogent-cabinet--agent-plist-value agent :active t))

   687	(defun ogent-cabinet-list-sessions (directory &optional agent-slug)
   688	  "Return Cabinet sessions under DIRECTORY.
   689	When AGENT-SLUG is non-nil, only return sessions for that agent."
   690	  (let* ((root (ogent-cabinet--directory directory))
   691	         (slugs (if agent-slug
   692	                    (list agent-slug)
   693	                  (ogent-cabinet-list-agents root)))
   694	         sessions)
   695	    (dolist (slug slugs)
   696	      (let ((sessions-dir (ogent-cabinet-sessions-directory root slug)))
   697	        (when (file-directory-p sessions-dir)
   698	          (dolist (file (directory-files sessions-dir t "\\.org\\'"))
   699	            (when (file-regular-p file)
   700	              (push (ogent-cabinet-read-session-file file slug) sessions))))))
   701	    (seq-sort
   702	     (lambda (left right)
   703	       (string> (or (plist-get left :finished) "")
   704	                (or (plist-get right :finished) "")))
   705	     sessions)))
   706
   707	(defun ogent-cabinet--hidden-path-p (root file)
   708	  "Return non-nil when FILE below ROOT is internal Cabinet plumbing."
   709	  (let ((relative (file-relative-name file root)))
   710	    (string-match-p
   711	     "\\`\\(?:\\.git\\|\\.cabinet-state\\|\\.agents/.conversations\\)/"
   712	     relative)))
   713
   714	(defun ogent-cabinet-org-files (directory)
   715	  "Return Cabinet Org files under DIRECTORY."
   716	  (let* ((root (ogent-cabinet--directory directory))
   717	         (files (directory-files-recursively root "\\.org\\'")))
   718	    (seq-filter
   719	     (lambda (file)
   720	       (not (ogent-cabinet--hidden-path-p root file)))
   721	     files)))
   722
   723	(defun ogent-cabinet-record-metadata (file)
   724	  "Return metadata plist for the Cabinet Org record in FILE."
   725	  (with-temp-buffer
   726	    (insert-file-contents file nil 0 nil)
   727	    (org-mode)
   728	    (condition-case nil
   729	        (progn
   730	          (let ((heading (ogent-cabinet--first-heading-title)))
   731	            (list
   732	             :kind (cond
   733	                    ((org-entry-get nil "OGENT_CABINET") 'cabinet)
   734	                    ((org-entry-get nil "OGENT_AGENT") 'agent)
   735	                    ((org-entry-get nil "OGENT_JOB") 'job)
   736	                    ((org-entry-get nil "OGENT_SESSION") 'session)
   737	                    ((org-entry-get nil "OGENT_IMPORT") 'import)
   738	                    ((org-entry-get nil "OGENT_ISSUE_ID") 'issue-link)
   739	                    (t 'org))
   740	             :heading heading
   741	             :agent (or (ogent-cabinet--blank-to-nil
   742	                         (org-entry-get nil "OGENT_AGENT"))
   743	                        (ogent-cabinet--blank-to-nil
   744	                         (org-entry-get nil "OGENT_SLUG")))
   745	             :status (or (nth 2 (org-heading-components))
   746	                         (ogent-cabinet--blank-to-nil
   747	                          (org-entry-get nil "OGENT_STATUS")))
   748	             :tags (append (org-get-tags nil t)
   749	                           (ogent-cabinet--tags-from-string
   750	                            (org-entry-get nil "OGENT_TAGS")))
   751	             :archived (ogent-cabinet--truth-value
   752	                        (org-entry-get nil "OGENT_ARCHIVED"))
   753	             :issue-id (ogent-cabinet--blank-to-nil
   754	                        (org-entry-get nil "OGENT_ISSUE_ID"))
   755	             :assigned-worker (ogent-cabinet--blank-to-nil
   756	                               (org-entry-get nil "OGENT_ASSIGNED_WORKER")))))
   757	      (error (list :kind 'org :heading nil :tags nil)))))

   760	  "Return the Cabinet record kind represented by FILE."
   761	  (plist-get (ogent-cabinet-record-metadata file) :kind))

   763	(defun ogent-cabinet--record-matches-filters-p (metadata kind agent status tag archived)
   764	  "Return non-nil when METADATA matches supplied search filters."
   765	  (and (or (null kind) (eq (plist-get metadata :kind) kind))
   766	       (or (null agent) (equal (plist-get metadata :agent) agent))
   767	       (or (null status) (equal (plist-get metadata :status) status))
   768	       (or (null tag) (member tag (plist-get metadata :tags)))
   769	       (or (null archived)
   770	           (eq (plist-get metadata :archived)
   771	               (ogent-cabinet--truth-value archived)))))
   772
   773	(cl-defun ogent-cabinet-search-records
   774	    (directory query &key kind agent status tag archived)
   775	  "Return Cabinet search matches for QUERY under DIRECTORY.
   776	Optional filters narrow by KIND, AGENT, STATUS, TAG, and ARCHIVED state."
   777	  (let ((root (ogent-cabinet--directory directory))
   778	        (case-fold-search t)
   779	        (regexp (regexp-quote (or query "")))
   780	        results)
   781	    (unless (string-blank-p (or query ""))
   782	      (dolist (file (ogent-cabinet-org-files root))
   783	        (let ((metadata (ogent-cabinet-record-metadata file)))
   784	          (when (ogent-cabinet--record-matches-filters-p
   785	                 metadata kind agent status tag archived)
   786	            (let ((line-number 0))
   787	              (with-temp-buffer
   788	                (insert-file-contents file)
   789	                (goto-char (point-min))
   790	                (while (not (eobp))
   791	                  (setq line-number (1+ line-number))
   792	                  (let ((line (buffer-substring-no-properties
   793	                               (line-beginning-position)
   794	                               (line-end-position))))
   795	                    (when (string-match-p regexp line)
   796	                      (push (append
   797	                             (list :path file
   798	                                   :line line-number
   799	                                   :text (string-trim line))
   800	                             metadata)
   801	                            results)))
   802	                  (forward-line 1))))))))
   803	    (nreverse results)))
   804
   805	(defun ogent-cabinet--app-owner (root relative)
   806	  "Return owner metadata for app RELATIVE under ROOT."
   807	  (or
   808	   (seq-find
   809	    (lambda (session)
   810	      (member relative (plist-get session :app-paths)))
   811	    (ogent-cabinet-list-sessions root))
   812	   (let ((parts (split-string relative "/" t)))
   813	     (when (and (equal (car parts) ".agents") (cadr parts))
   814	       (list :agent (cadr parts))))))

    83	(defun ogent-cabinet-runner-normalize-provider (provider)
    84	  "Return canonical provider symbol for PROVIDER."
    85	  (let ((value (downcase (string-trim (format "%s" (or provider "codex"))))))
    86	    (cond
    87	     ((member value '("" "default" "codex" "codex-cli" "openai-codex"))
    88	      'codex)
    89	     ((member value '("claude" "claude-code" "anthropic" "anthropic-claude"))
    90	      'claude)
    91	     (t (intern value)))))

   100	       ((or (null workspace) (equal workspace "/")) root)

   102	       (t (expand-file-name workspace root)))))))

   123	(defun ogent-cabinet-runner--prompt (agent &optional job instruction)
   124	  "Return a CLI prompt from AGENT, optional JOB, and INSTRUCTION."
   125	  (string-join
   126	   (delq
   127	    nil
   128	    (list
   129	     (format "You are the Org Cabinet agent named %s."
   130	             (or (plist-get agent :name) (plist-get agent :slug) "agent"))
   131	     (when-let ((role (ogent-cabinet-runner--blank-to-nil
   132	                       (plist-get agent :role))))
   133	       (format "Role: %s" role))
   134	     (when-let ((body (ogent-cabinet-runner--blank-to-nil
   135	                       (plist-get agent :body))))
   136	       (format "Persona instructions:\n%s" body))
   137	     (when job
   138	       (format "Run this Cabinet job: %s."
   139	               (or (plist-get job :name) (plist-get job :id))))
   140	     (when-let ((job-body (and job
   141	                               (ogent-cabinet-runner--blank-to-nil
   142	                                (plist-get job :body)))))
   143	       (format "Job instructions:\n%s" job-body))
   144	     (when-let ((user-instruction
   145	                 (ogent-cabinet-runner--blank-to-nil instruction)))
   146	       (format "User instruction:\n%s" user-instruction))))
   147	   "\n\n"))

   149	(defun ogent-cabinet-runner--append-option (args option value)
   150	  "Append OPTION and VALUE to ARGS when VALUE is nonblank."
   151	  (if (ogent-cabinet-runner--blank-to-nil value)
   152	      (append args (list option value))
   153	    args))

   155	(cl-defun ogent-cabinet-runner-plan
   156	    (directory agent-slug &key job-id instruction)
   157	  "Return a process plan for AGENT-SLUG under DIRECTORY.
   158	JOB-ID selects a recurring job.  INSTRUCTION supplies an ad hoc prompt."
   159	  (let* ((candidate (ogent-cabinet--directory directory))
   160	         (root (file-truename
   161	                (ogent-cabinet--directory
   162	                 (or (ogent-cabinet-find-root candidate)
   163	                     candidate))))
   164	         (agent (ogent-cabinet-read-agent root agent-slug))
   165	         (job (when job-id
   166	                (ogent-cabinet-validate-job
   167	                 (ogent-cabinet-read-job root agent-slug job-id))))
   168	         (provider (ogent-cabinet-runner-normalize-provider
   169	                    (or (ogent-cabinet-runner--effective agent job :provider)
   170	                        (plist-get agent :provider))))
   171	         (workspace (ogent-cabinet-runner--workspace
   172	                     root
   173	                     (if (and job (plist-get job :workspace))
   174	                         (plist-put (copy-sequence agent)
   175	                                    :workspace
   176	                                    (plist-get job :workspace))
   177	                       agent)))
   178	         (prompt (ogent-cabinet-runner--prompt agent job instruction))
   179	         (model (ogent-cabinet-runner--effective agent job :model))
   180	         (permission-mode (or (ogent-cabinet-runner--blank-to-nil
   181	                               (plist-get agent :permission-mode))
   182	                              ogent-cabinet-runner-claude-permission-mode))
   183	         (session-file (ogent-cabinet-runner--session-file
   184	                        root agent-slug job-id)))
   185	    (unless (file-directory-p workspace)
   186	      (user-error "Cabinet agent workspace not found: %s" workspace))
   187	    (pcase provider
   188	      ('codex
   189	       (let ((args (list "--ask-for-approval"
   190	                         ogent-cabinet-runner-codex-approval
   191	                         "exec"
   192	                         "--cd" workspace
   193	                         "--sandbox" ogent-cabinet-runner-codex-sandbox)))
   194	         (when ogent-cabinet-runner-codex-skip-git-repo-check
   195	           (setq args (append args (list "--skip-git-repo-check"))))
   196	         (setq args (ogent-cabinet-runner--append-option args "--model" model))
   197	         (list :provider provider
   198	               :program ogent-cabinet-codex-executable
   199	               :args (append args (list "-"))
   200	               :prompt prompt
   201	               :stdin prompt
   202	               :root root
   203	               :workspace workspace
   204	               :agent agent
   205	               :job job
   206	               :session-file session-file)))
   207	      ('claude
   208	       (let ((args (list "-p"
   209	                         "--permission-mode" permission-mode
   210	                         "--add-dir" root)))
   211	         (setq args (ogent-cabinet-runner--append-option args "--model" model))
   212	         (list :provider provider
   213	               :program ogent-cabinet-claude-executable
   214	               :args (append args (list prompt))
   215	               :prompt prompt
   216	               :stdin nil
   217	               :root root
   218	               :workspace workspace
   219	               :agent agent
   220	               :job job
   221	               :session-file session-file)))
   222	      (_
   223	       (user-error "Unsupported Cabinet agent provider: %s" provider)))))
   224
   225	(defun ogent-cabinet-runner--org-src-text (text)
   226	  "Return TEXT escaped for insertion in an Org src block."
   227	  (let ((escaped
   228	         (mapconcat
   229	          (lambda (line)
   230	            (let ((case-fold-search t))
   231	              (if (string-match-p "\\`[ \t]*#\\+end_src\\_>" line)
   232	                  (concat "," line)
   233	                line)))
   234	          (split-string (or text "") "\n")
   235	          "\n")))
   236	    (cond
   237	     ((string-empty-p escaped) "")
   238	     ((string-suffix-p "\n" escaped) escaped)
   239	     (t (concat escaped "\n")))))
